CREATE OR ALTER PROCEDURE GetNearestPostCode @east int, @north int
AS
DECLARE @ResultValue VARCHAR(10)
BEGIN 
  SELECT MA_DIA_CHI ,TEN_DIA_CHI , SQRT(
    POWER(CONVERT(bigint,(TOA_DO_DONG - @east)), 2) +
    POWER(CONVERT(bigint,(TOA_DO_BAC - @north)), 2)) AS distance
FROM DIA_CHI WHERE SQRT(
    POWER(CONVERT(bigint,(TOA_DO_DONG - @east)), 2) +
    POWER(CONVERT(bigint,(TOA_DO_BAC - @north)), 2))  < 100000 ORDER BY distance

END
GO
CREATE OR ALTER trigger UpdateDonGia_ChiTietDonHang
ON dbo.CHI_TIET_DON_HANG
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS 
BEGIN

    --
    -- Check if this is an INSERT, UPDATE or DELETE Action.
    -- 
    DECLARE @gia as int;
	DECLARE @machitietdonhang as int;
	DECLARE @madonhang as int;
	
	SET @madonhang = (select MA_DON_HANG from inserted)
	SET @machitietdonhang = (select id from inserted)
	SET @gia = (select SAN_PHAM.GIA_SP FROM inserted join SAN_PHAM on inserted.MA_SP = SAN_PHAM.MA_SP where SAN_PHAM.MA_SP = inserted.MA_SP)
	if(@gia is not null)
	UPDATE CHI_TIET_DON_HANG
	SET DON_GIA = SO_LUONG * @gia
	where Id = @machitietdonhang

	UPDATE DON_HANG
	SET TongTien = (SELECT SUM(DON_GIA) FROM CHI_TIET_DON_HANG where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang)
	where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang


END;
GO


CREATE OR ALTER trigger UpdateDonGia_ChiTietDonHang_Delete
ON dbo.CHI_TIET_DON_HANG
AFTER DELETE
AS 
BEGIN

    --
    -- Check if this is an INSERT, UPDATE or DELETE Action.
    -- 
    DECLARE @gia as int;
	DECLARE @machitietdonhang as int;
	DECLARE @madonhang as int;
	
	SET @madonhang = (select MA_DON_HANG from deleted)
	SET @machitietdonhang = (select id from deleted)
	SET @gia = (select SAN_PHAM.GIA_SP FROM deleted join SAN_PHAM on deleted.MA_SP = SAN_PHAM.MA_SP where SAN_PHAM.MA_SP = deleted.MA_SP)
	
	

	UPDATE DON_HANG
	SET TongTien = (SELECT SUM(DON_GIA) FROM CHI_TIET_DON_HANG where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang)
	where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang


END;
GO


CREATE OR ALTER trigger UpdateTongTien_DonHang
ON dbo.DON_HANG
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE, DELETE
AS 
BEGIN
	 DECLARE @gia as int;
	DECLARE @madonhang as int;
	IF EXISTS (SELECT *
               FROM deleted
               )
	BEGIN
		SET @madonhang = (select MA_DON_HANG from deleted)
		SET @gia = (SELECT SUM(DON_GIA) FROM CHI_TIET_DON_HANG where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang)
		if(@gia is not null)
		UPDATE DON_HANG
		SET TongTien = @gia
		where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang
	END
	IF EXISTS (SELECT *
               FROM inserted
               )
	BEGIN
		SET @madonhang = (select MA_DON_HANG from inserted)
		SET @gia = (SELECT SUM(DON_GIA) FROM CHI_TIET_DON_HANG where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang)
		if(@gia is not null)
		UPDATE DON_HANG
		SET TongTien = @gia
		where MA_DON_HANG = @madonhang
	END

END
GO
CREATE OR ALTER trigger UpdateDonGia_ChiTietGioHang
ON dbo.CHI_TIET_GIO_HANG
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS 
BEGIN

    --
    -- Check if this is an INSERT, UPDATE or DELETE Action.
    -- 
    DECLARE @gia as int;
	DECLARE @machitietdonhang as int;
	DECLARE @magiohang as int;
	
	SET @magiohang = (select MA_GIO_HANG from inserted)
	SET @machitietdonhang = (select id from inserted)
	SET @gia = (select SAN_PHAM.GIA_SP FROM inserted join SAN_PHAM on inserted.MA_SP = SAN_PHAM.MA_SP where SAN_PHAM.MA_SP = inserted.MA_SP)
	

	UPDATE GIO_HANG
	SET TONG_TIEN = (SELECT SUM(GIA_SP * SO_LUONG) FROM CHI_TIET_GIO_HANG join SAN_PHAM on CHI_TIET_GIO_HANG.MA_SP = SAN_PHAM.MA_SP where MA_GIO_HANG = @magiohang)
	where MA_GIO_HANG = @magiohang


END;
GO


CREATE OR ALTER trigger UpdateDonGia_ChiTietGioHang_Delete
ON dbo.CHI_TIET_GIO_HANG
AFTER DELETE
AS 
BEGIN

    --
    -- Check if this is an INSERT, UPDATE or DELETE Action.
    -- 
    DECLARE @gia as int;
	DECLARE @machitietdonhang as int;
	DECLARE @magiohang as int;
	
	SET @magiohang = (select MA_GIO_HANG from deleted)
	SET @machitietdonhang = (select id from deleted)
	SET @gia = (select SAN_PHAM.GIA_SP FROM deleted join SAN_PHAM on deleted.MA_SP = SAN_PHAM.MA_SP where SAN_PHAM.MA_SP = deleted.MA_SP)
	

	UPDATE GIO_HANG
	SET TONG_TIEN = (SELECT SUM(GIA_SP * SO_LUONG) FROM CHI_TIET_GIO_HANG join SAN_PHAM on CHI_TIET_GIO_HANG.MA_SP = SAN_PHAM.MA_SP where MA_GIO_HANG = @magiohang)
	where MA_GIO_HANG = @magiohang


END;
GO





CREATE OR ALTER trigger Update_DanhGia
ON dbo.DANH_GIA
AFTER INSERT, UPDATE
AS 
BEGIN

    --
    -- Check if this is an INSERT, UPDATE or DELETE Action.
    -- 
    
	DECLARE @masp as int;
	
	SET @masp = (select MA_SAN_PHAM from inserted)
	
	UPDATE SAN_PHAM
	SET SoLuotDanhGia = SoLuotDanhGia + 1
	where MA_SP = @masp;
	UPDATE SAN_PHAM
	SET TrungBinhSao = (select SUM(SAO) from DANH_GIA where MA_SAN_PHAM = @masp)*1.00 / SoLuotDanhGia 
	where MA_SP = @masp



END;
GO


CREATE OR ALTER trigger Delete_DanhGia
ON dbo.DANH_GIA
AFTER DELETE
AS 
BEGIN

    --
    -- Check if this is an INSERT, UPDATE or DELETE Action.
    -- 
    
	DECLARE @masp as int;
	
	SET @masp = (select MA_SAN_PHAM from deleted)
	
	UPDATE SAN_PHAM
	SET SoLuotDanhGia = SoLuotDanhGia - 1
	where MA_SP = @masp;
	UPDATE SAN_PHAM
	SET TrungBinhSao = (select SUM(SAO) from DANH_GIA where MA_SAN_PHAM = @masp)*1.00  / SoLuotDanhGia 
	where MA_SP = @masp



END;
GO
